 In the 64th match of the sixth edition of the Indian Premier League (IPL), Chennai Super Kings at Chennai's MA Chidambaram Stadium would like to strengthen their position at the top by beating Delhi Daredevils
 pichley teen muqablon main super kings ko do main haar mili he, baavjood iske ve abhi bhi nau tiimon kii ankatalika main sheersh par kaayam hai
 The Super Kings have won 10 out of 14 matches so far and remain the top team with 20 points
 haalanki rajasthan royles ke bhi itane hi ank hai lekin net ran rate kam hone kii vajah se vah duusare sthaan par he
 The Delhi Daredevils, on the other hand, have had a dismal performance in this IPL season and have managed to win only three out of 13 matches, while losing 10 matches
 dairedevills chah ankon ke saath nau tiimon kii ankatalika main aathven sthaan par he

 dairedevills ke liye yah match sammaan bachaane vaala match hoga

 super kings ne ab tak 14 maichon main 10 main jeet darj kii he or 20 ankon ke saath sheersh team bani hui he

 ab tak ke pradarshan ke aadhaar par super kings or dairedevills kii koi tulana nahin he, lekin dairedevills is myne main khatarnaak ho sakate hai kyonki ab unke paas khone ke liye kuch bhi nahin he
 For the Daredevils, this match will be an honor-saving match
 chennai main hone vaale is match main dairedevills ke liye haalanki captain mahela jayavardhane nahin khel sakenge, kyonki rajya main srilankai khilaadiyon kaa virodh chal rahaa he

 1
 ISRO was founded in 1969 on Independence Day
 iske sansthaapak dow
 Vikram Sarabhai was
 2
 The SLV-3 was India's first indigenous satellite launch vehicle
 is project ke diarector purv raashtrapati apije abdul kalam the
 3
 isro kam kharch main kaam karata he
 According to a report, isro's 40-year expenditure is equivalent to nasa's six-month expenditure
 4
 ISRO has 13 centers in various cities in India
 5
 isro's Mars mission is said to be the cheapest
 ab tak is par kareeb450 karod rupee kharch hue hai
 6
 bharat pehla aisa desh he jisane isro kii madad se pehle hi prayaas main mars tak pahunchane main kamyaabi hasil kar lee
 7
 kaha jaataa he ki isro ek aisa orgenigeshan he jisamen sabase adhik bachaler kaam karte hai
 8
 isro ne ab tak 23 pieselvi satellite launch kiya he
 9
 isro ne 65 bhartiya satellite ke saath-saath 29 videshi satellite kii lonching bhi kii he
 10
 isro kaa fasebuk pej bhi he

 pej ke kareeb 13 lakh folbers hai

 himachal pradesh state act, 1970 paarit hone ke baad yah desh kaa 18waan rajya bana
 Earlier it was officially a union territory
 ye hai duniya kii sabase lambii nadiyaan

 congress ke diggaj netaa yashavanth singh parmaar is rajya ke pehle mukhyamantri bane

 60 lakh thi, jo saal 2015 main 68

 dilli police ke nireekshak anil sharma ne yachika main kaha he ki is sanshodhan ke baad police kii kaary kshamta prabhavit hogi
 Amendments made in 2013 Section 197 of the CRPC mandated the approval of the concerned department's authority before prosecuting any government employee or officer, but amended in 2013, government employees or officers involved in cases of crimes against women This compulsion to register Paramukdama was abolished
 prabhavit hogi kaam karne kii kshamtadilli police ke nireekshak anil sharma ne is sanshodhan ko chunauti dete huehai courtmen janhit yachika daayar kii he, jis par hai court sunwaayee kar rahaa he
 The police told the High Court that by changing the law and arranging to prosecute government employees in cases of alleged crimes against women without sanction, it would be easier for the wrongdoers to make false allegations against the policemen
 isse police kii kaam karne kii kshamta prabhavit hogi
